_raw  = base64.b64decode(_DICT_B64)
_text = gzip.decompress(_raw).decode("utf-8")
WORD_SET = set(w for w in _text.split("
") if w)

def _get_tg(w):
    n = 2 if len(w) < 3 else 3
    p = " " + w + " "
    return [p[i:i+n] for i in range(len(p) - n + 1)]

TG_IDX = defaultdict(list)
for _w in WORD_SET:
    for _tg in _get_tg(_w):
        TG_IDX[_tg].append(_w)
TG_IDX = dict(TG_IDX)

print(f"Seeds:    {len(SEEDS)} sentences")
print(f"Targets:  {len(targets_proc)} sentences")
print(f"Dict:     {len(WORD_SET):,} words")
print(f"Trigrams: {len(TG_IDX):,} entries")

=== CELL 4 ===
# Cell 4 -- Run simulation (multiprocessing, 2 workers)
import multiprocessing, time

SCALARS    = [0.25, 0.5, 1.0, 1.5]
N_RUNS     = 10
POP_SIZE   = 1000
N_CHILDREN = 10
MAX_GENS   = 500
EXIT_FIT   = 0.99
EXIT_COUNT = 1000

def _worker(args):
    scalar, use_ecm, run_idx = args
    run_id = f's{scalar}_ecm{int(use_ecm)}_{run_idx:02d}'
    return run_one(
        run_id, scalar, use_ecm,
        targets_proc, SEEDS, WORD_SET, TG_IDX,
        pop_size=POP_SIZE, n_children=N_CHILDREN, max_gens=MAX_GENS,
        exit_fit=EXIT_FIT, exit_count=EXIT_COUNT
    )

jobs = [
    (scalar, use_ecm, run_idx)
    for scalar  in SCALARS
    for use_ecm in [True, False]
    for run_idx in range(N_RUNS)
]
print(f"{len(jobs)} total runs  ({len(SCALARS)} scalars x 2 conditions x {N_RUNS} runs)")

t0 = time.time()
all_rows = []

with multiprocessing.Pool(processes=2) as pool:
    for i, result in enumerate(pool.imap_unordered(_worker, jobs), 1):
        all_rows.extend(result)
        elapsed = time.time() - t0
        print(f"  [{i}/{len(jobs)}] done -- {elapsed/60:.1f} min elapsed", flush=True)

print(f"
Complete. {len(all_rows):,} rows total. {(time.time()-t0)/60:.1f} min.")

=== CELL 5 ===
# Cell 5 -- Save results to CSV and download
import csv, io
from google.colab import files

fieldnames = ['run_id','generation','mutation_scalar','use_ecm',
              'mean_fitness','max_fitness','n_full_fit']

buf = io.StringIO()
writer = csv.DictWriter(buf, fieldnames=fieldnames)
writer.writeheader()
writer.writerows(all_rows)

filename = "BFG_Replication_50-50_ecm80_full.csv"
with open(filename, "w", newline="") as f:
    f.write(buf.getvalue())

print(f"Saved {len(all_rows):,} rows to {filename}")
files.download(filename)
